EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceGiveHelp=更改所选玩家之间的提供帮助同盟状态。默认情况下，假如你直接输入“AllianceGiveHelp”，所有的玩家将会响应你单位所发出的呼叫帮助。 /// Changes the GiveHelp alliance state between the selected players. By default, if you just type AllianceGiveHelp, all players will respond to calls for help from your units.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AlliancePassive=更改所选玩家之间的被动同盟状态。那些对你而言不是被动的玩家，其攻击意图将被视为有敌意的。 /// Changes the Passive alliance state between the selected players. Players that you are not passive with will be considered hostile for attacking purposes.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AlliancePushable=更改所选玩家之间的可推动同盟状态。这控制了一个玩家的单位是否能够穿过另一个玩家的单位，将他们推开。 /// Changes the Pushable alliance state between the selected players. This controls whether a player’s units will move through another player’s units, pushing them out of the way.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceSeekHelp=更改所选玩家之间的寻求帮助同盟状态。控制了一个玩家的单位是否向指定目标玩家呼叫帮助。目标玩家可选择响应或不响应，这取决于它的提供帮助同盟设定。 /// Changes the SeekHelp alliance state between the selected players. Controls whether a player’s units call for help to the specified target player. The target player can choose to respond or not, depending on its GiveHelp alliance setting.
EDSTR_CHEATDESC_AllianceSpend=更改所选玩家之间的花费同盟状态。允许和你共享资源的玩家可以花费你的资金来购买物品。
